3a1(kha): y/ dang / lu ba dang / thug pa dang / ldeg pa dang / tshem pa dang / mi bde ba sna tshigs byungno// gsung dun bon gyi bstan pa bshig gozer ba'i phra gragsso// srid pa'i ba /

3a6(kha): bstan pa rtsod/ khyed la sprul pa ci tsam yod/ bdud srin d kyi sdong grogs gyis/ zhes smras so// khye'u smras pa/ lam nor ma log ste/ bdud srin 'tshogs par thos/ ngo mtshar 
3b1(kha): / che ba'i sems/ lhad de lta ra 'ong / su yin mi shes sems/ chu ltham rgyal ba mtchod/ gsang ba 'dus pa dang / d lha gngana yo// snang mun gnyis kyi bstan pa d// kbyed kyi rtsod pa /

3b3(kha): kyi gnas su 'ong / de skad smras nas/ bdu srin mkhar na du byung ste/ khrom tshogs kyi dbu ro sna tshogs kyi khri steng na nabs ma'i gur du bzhugs shig zhal 'dzum par mdzad nas/ 
3b4(kha): de'i che stag lha me 'bar dang / yongs su dag pa dang / mi lus bsam legs dang / ye shes snying po dang bzhi yang / khye'u chung bzhi rung sprul nas/ mkhar gyi phyi rol du byung nas smras pa/ 
3b5(kha): bdu srin dmag tshogs khyed cag rnams d kyi gcen po gang du song zhes smras pas/ gab pa lo dor gyis smras pa/ gcen po d kyi mkhar na yod/ khyed cag gar 'gro ca la 'ong /

4a1(kha): sdeg grogs dmag pung gyis/ bgyogs par 'hud la mi rgyung na/ mkhar gyi na du gsal khrid ces smras'o// the' bzhes smras pa/ pa gcig bu la ming gcig go
4a2(kha): gcen po mkhar gyi nang du khrid/ de bzhi me khrid ci yi phyir/ sding grogs dmag dpung 'dzud pa ni/ gcen pos byed na de kyang bya/ da lta khas len med/ gnod sbyien khyed lang rgyal 
4a3(kha): che/ lhad mo ba la dmag gyis zer/ khyed kyi zer ba kha na med/ sdong grogs byed dam gnod par byed/ rang gi 'dod pa'i kha na med/ las kyi dbang bskur so sor 'ong / zhes smras nas

4a6(kha): 'dus pa de/ sems can yongs la brtsi sems che/ g.yung drung bon gyi bstan pa de/ sems can thams cad bde la bkod/ de la rtsod pa ma byed cig// d kyi rtsod pa mi byed do// 
4b1(kha): byas kyang thub par mi 'gyur ro// khams gsum sems can bsad pa nas/ tsen la rtsod pa byas na sdig/ 'dir sdug phyi mar ngan song brgyud/ snying grogs lags kyis go bar gyis/

4b6(kha): pas bdud srin rnams dbang du bsdus par dgongs nas/ dbal gss sngam par sku sprul te/ dbu dgu phyag bco brgyad pa zhabs bzhi ru bsgrad pa/ sku la gdug pa'i chas sna tshogs 
5a1(kha): kyes brgyan p/ subm sed pa'i rgyal mo lha zamtsan dug m 'brel bar sul te/ kbyeng khyi bi rgyal che mtchog kyang / ye she sems dpa' rnam spyan dpa/

5a3(kha): gsungs so// bso oM a thun nyi lo yo thun sungs so thad d thun/ to yo brag znan/ ge du drig nan/ a mu drig znhan/ tsa ba brig nan/ de basad brig znan/ a rge ra ta /

6a1(kha): sems nyid thugs rje ye shes sku/ de don gsal bar ston pa'i gsang bsngags tsogs las tog 'dzoms gzungs/ 'di don gsal bar rtogs gyur na/ 'khrul rtog /

18b6(19): rnying du sems pa'i nges shes las/ 'phrin las g.yel med sgyong mdzad pa'i/ mchog sprul 'o zer thyin sa gtcos/ dag zhus yig bskar bris mkhan dang / lhag sems nus thugs mnyam threl ngang / 
19a1(19): // las non bye po thals ca dang / bos nams tshogs gyi rnying po che/ gya la'i bar las len pa ang / rig gkhung cho srog glob pa'i che/ ngos po'i mthun rkyen gtong pho pa'i/ 'byor / 
19a2(19): ldag yon gyi bag bcas la/ legs gsol yi rang phrul tsal gyis/ dge ba'i tshal pa mnyal 'gyur na/ rnying nas mongon par bste dang lhan/ gsung gi 'khrin las yel ba yi/ drubs chen dge / 
19a3(19): ba'i rtsa ba 'dis/ br sob yon bdag bcas pa yi/ bar chod rkyen ngan mthar bcil nas/ bsam don lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / mthar yang god ma'i zhing khams su/ bdag gzhan don gnyis byang 
19a4(19): chub nas/ chabs cig mongn sangs rgyas par thog/ lung rtogs bstan pa'i rnying po gang / sre pa'i mthar yang gnas pa ang / res le bstan 'dzin kyes bu'i tshogs/ 'gro na gegs me lhag grub 
19a5(19): theg/ yangs pa'i zhing khams thams cad du/ nang mtshon lu ge rgyun chad nas/ 'gro rnams zhi bod' pal yen la/ longs su spyodg pa'i bgra nyis thog/ ces pa'i 'bel dtsem chen shig 'di nyid gsung 
19a6(19): dung ben gyi gnasa dpal ldan khri brtan nad bu'i rce nas slob dpen gyi ming 'dzin tshangs pa bstan 'dzin 'og pas brag/ rnyen bris te phrul bo'// zhus bgrigs chan pa'i gsal basn// gang gsal le'u / 
19b1(19): chan chag ngo sprod so seMr zhus bzhin/ le' chan gong 'ag de rnams kyi ma dpe la bres pa'i chad nad dang / mngon gsal can gyi rkyen ma then degs la za brkangs byas pa las/ gang byung gi bcoes thal ma byas pad// ni / 
19b2(19): bzhi mdzed lnga'i dse rnying phyegs bgrigs / kyo a grangs apad zhus bgrigs byas yod kyang ddung ma rtegs dbang gis chad lhagsegs yod nges te/ spyi la rbbyad sngen lo nga lnga brgya ldhag nas gangs can bad / 
19b3(19): kyi yul du yi go' par zang 'jzugs bsgyun dang // pe gzhi legs bsgrigs byas pa'i 'grels spel yengs khyab byed srel dad zen na'ang / gsung dung boen gyi dpe gzho' bsdu bgrigs byed pa' ga rkabs kyi thad spug de tsam 
19b4(19): byung med pas/ 'dod phyogs la nyams myeng dang lag len segs la mig nes len gzhi dken pas gel cha gsad du yin pa dang / ges su de zhus bgrigs pa che yang mkhyen dpyed dab 'byams pa min chad/ 'di' thad mthun / 
19b5(19): rkyen zung la 'gal rkyen mang ba'i gseb ru dal brling 'grig sa dang la byung na/ phyegs gang so'i ched yug dang gnas sangs tsha las brgal ba'i legs ma zhig then thabs med pas/ de lcugs kyis rjes su gzigs mkhan / 
19b6(19): rnam pas 'di la dg rkyen thad ye bsrang yeng nges gnang de che zhing / 'di yi byas pa 'dis kyang suad du g.sung dung ben gyi lung gi bstan pa don po me gsal dag 'grig po'i zhabs zhu' grabs bsdegs tsam du 'gyur snyam che ba / 
20a1(19): / a nan/ a n // co/ 
20a2(19): nyin/ byung po sdang chen dgon go mdz dpe zhus tshan pas// 
20a3(19): kar mo zen a'i rgyas ci/ nagcozer pa'i thab so/
